<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Take Time<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Divine Life Society Publication: </b><a href="file:///C:/Users/Ravi/AppData/Local/Temp/(Dec%2012,2014)%20Spiritual%20Message%20for%20the%20Day%20%E2%80%93%20Take%20Time%20by%20Sri%20Swami%20Chidananda"><b>Message of Swami Chidananda to Mankind</b></a><b> by Sri Swami <a name="_VPID_65">Chidananda<o:p></o:p></a></b></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to THINK... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the source of power. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to PLAY... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the secret of perpetual youth. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to READ... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the fountain of wisdom </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to PRAY... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the greatest power on earth. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to LOVE and BE LOVED... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is a God-given privilege. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to BE FRIENDLY... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the road to happiness. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to LAUGH... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the music of the soul. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to GIVE... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is too short a day to be selfish. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to WORK... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the price of success. </span></p>
<p style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take Time to DO CHARITY... </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> It is the key to heaven. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><span class="MsoHyperlink" style="line-height: normal;"><b>Excerpts from: </b></span><b style="line-height: normal; font-size: 11px;">Take Time - </b><a href="file:///C:/Users/G/Dropbox/DLS%20Satsang%20meditation%20session/Dec%202014/(Dec%2012,2014)%20Spiritual%20Message%20for%20the%20Day%20%E2%80%93%20Take%20Time%20by%20Sri%20Swami%20Chidananda" style="line-height: normal; font-size: 11px;"><b>Message of Swami Chidananda to Mankind</b></a><b style="line-height: normal; font-size: 11px;"> by Sri Swami Chidananda</b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">If you would like to purchase the print edition, visit: </span><strong style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/download/download.htm"><span style="color: #0000ff;" color="#0066cc">The Divine Life Society E-Bookstore</span></a></span></strong></p>
